To do this, we need to subtract the percentage change in the price of petroleum oil from 100%.\nSo, the percentage change in the consumer's petroleum bill is:\n100% - (y% x (X + 10% - X))\nNow, we can plug in the values we have found so far:\n100% - (y% x (X + 10% - X)) = 100% - (y% x (X + 10% - X))\nSimplifying this equation, we get:\n100% - (y% x (X + 10% - X)) = 100% - (y% x (X + 10%) - (X + 10%))\n= 100% - (y% x 10%) - (y% x 10%)\n= 90%\n\nSo, the probability that the answer is correct is ###0.9###.")
